* Deno file system APIs in edge functions were aligned with the production environment and are now also not available anymore locally.
* drop node 14.16 and 14.17 ([#5602](https://github.com/netlify/cli/issues/5602))

## [6.0.0](https://www.github.com/netlify/cli/compare/v5.4.16...v6.0.0) (2021-08-04)


### ⚠ BREAKING CHANGES

The `deploy` command will now look for a functions cache created by the `build` command and deploy any existing function archives. You can disable this feature with `--skip-functions-cache` flag, which will tell the CLI to create fresh archives as part of the deployment.

```
netlify deploy --skip-functions-cache
```

## [4.0.0](https://www.github.com/netlify/cli/compare/v3.39.4...v4.0.0) (2021-06-30)


### ⚠ BREAKING CHANGES

* **deps:** The `aws-sdk` npm package is no longer included with the Netlify CLI. If your functions use this module, you should add it to your project dependencies by running `npm install aws-sdk --save` or `yarn add aws-sdk`.
